There's no universal, portable way to define an agent that works across Claude Code, OpenAI, LangChain, CrewAI, and AutoGen. \u003cstrong\u003egitagent\u003c/strong\u003e fixes that.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGit-native\u003c/strong\u003e — Version control, branching, diffing, and collaboration built in\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFramework-agnostic\u003c/strong\u003e — Export to any framework with adapters\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCompliance-ready\u003c/strong\u003e — First-class support for FINRA, Federal Reserve, SEC, and segregation of duties\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eComposable\u003c/strong\u003e — Agents can extend, depend on, and delegate to other agents\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe Standard\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-the-standard\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: The Standard\" href=\"#the-standard\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYour repository becomes your agent. Drop these files into any git repo and it becomes a portable, framework-agnostic agent definition — everything else (CLI, adapters, patterns) builds on top of it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"my-agent/\n│\n│   # ── Core Identity (required) ──────────────────────────\n├── agent.yaml              # Manifest — name, version, model, skills, tools, compliance\n├── SOUL.md                 # Identity, personality, communication style, values\n│\n│   # ── Behavior \u0026amp; Rules ──────────────────────────────────\n├── RULES.md                # Hard constraints, must-always/must-never, safety boundaries\n├── DUTIES.md               # Segregation of duties policy and role boundaries\n├── AGENTS.md               # Framework-agnostic fallback instructions\n│\n│   # ── Capabilities ──────────────────────────────────────\n├── skills/                 # Reusable capability modules (SKILL.md + scripts)\n│   └── code-review/\n│       ├── SKILL.md\n│       └── review.sh\n├── tools/                  # MCP-compatible tool definitions (YAML schemas)\n├── workflows/              # Multi-step procedures/playbooks\n│\n│   # ── Knowledge \u0026amp; Memory ────────────────────────────────\n├── knowledge/              # Reference documents the agent can consult\n├── memory/                 # Persistent cross-session memory\n│   └── runtime/            # Live agent state (dailylog.md, context.md)\n│\n│   # ── Lifecycle \u0026amp; Ops ───────────────────────────────────\n├── hooks/                  # Lifecycle event handlers (bootstrap.md, teardown.md)\n├── config/                 # Environment-specific overrides\n├── compliance/             # Regulatory compliance artifacts\n│\n│   # ── Composition ───────────────────────────────────────\n├── agents/                 # Sub-agent definitions (recursive structure)\n│   └── fact-checker/\n│       ├── agent.yaml\n│       ├── SOUL.md\n│       └── DUTIES.md       # This agent's role, permissions, boundaries\n├── examples/               # Calibration interactions (few-shot)\n│\n│   # ── Runtime ───────────────────────────────────────────\n└── .gitagent/              # Runtime state (gitignored)\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003emy-agent/\n│\n│   # ── Core Identity (required) ──────────────────────────\n├── agent.yaml              # Manifest — name, version, model, skills, tools, compliance\n├── SOUL.md                 # Identity, personality, communication style, values\n│\n│   # ── Behavior \u0026amp; Everything else is optional — add what you need, ignore the rest.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" a critical process end-to-end. Define roles (\u003ccode\u003emaker\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003echecker\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eexecutor\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eauditor\u003c/code\u003e), a conflict matrix (which roles can't be the same agent), and handoff workflows — all in \u003ccode\u003eagent.yaml\u003c/code\u003e + \u003ccode\u003eDUTIES.md\u003c/code\u003e. The validator catches violations before deployment.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"compliance:\n  segregation_of_duties:\n    roles:\n      - id: maker\n        description: Creates proposals\n        permissions: [create, submit]\n      - id: checker\n        description: Reviews and approves\n        permissions: [review, approve, reject]\n    conflicts:\n      - [maker, checker]         # maker cannot approve own work\n    assignments:\n YAML. Chain \u003ccode\u003eskill:\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eagent:\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003etool:\u003c/code\u003e steps with \u003ccode\u003edepends_on\u003c/code\u003e ordering, \u003ccode\u003e${{ }}\u003c/code\u003e template data flow, and per-step \u003ccode\u003eprompt:\u003c/code\u003e overrides. Every run follows the same path — no LLM discretion on execution order.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"name: code-review-flow\ndescription: Full code review pipeline\ntriggers:\n  - pull_request\n\nsteps:\n  lint:\n    skill: static-analysis\n    inputs:\n      path: ${{ trigger.changed_files }}\n\n  review:\n    agent: code-reviewer\n    depends_on: [lint]\n    prompt: |\n      Focus on security and performance.\n      Flag any use of eval() or raw SQL.\n    inputs:\n      findings: ${{ steps.lint.outputs.issues }}\n\n  test:\n    tool: bash\n    depends_on: [lint]\n    inputs:\n      command: \u0026quot;npm test -- --coverage\u0026quot;\n\n  report:\n    skill: review-summary\n    depends_on: [review, test]\n    conditions:\n      - ${{ steps.review.outputs.severity != 'none' }}\n    inputs:\n      review: ${{ steps.review.outputs.comments }}\n      coverage: ${{ steps.test.outputs.report }}\n\nerror_handling:\n  on_failure: notify\n  channel: \u0026quot;#eng-reviews\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003epath\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e${{ trigger.changed_files }}\u003c/span\u003e\n\n  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003ereview\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003etest\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003etool\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003ebash\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003edepends_on\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e[lint]\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003einputs\u003c/span\u003e:\n      \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003ecommand\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003enpm test -- --coverage\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003ereview-summary\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003edepends_on\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e[review, test]\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003econditions\u003c/span\u003e:\n      - \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e${{ steps.review.outputs.severity != 'none' }}\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan    \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003ecoverage\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e${{ steps.test.outputs.report }}\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePorting Framework Agents to GitAgent\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-porting-framework-agents-to-gitagent\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Porting Framework Agents to GitAgent\" href=\"#porting-framework-agents-to-gitagent\"\u003e\u003csvg data-component=\"Octicon\" class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAgents built in frameworks like NVIDIA AIQ, LangGraph, or CrewAI have their identity split across config files, Jinja2 templates, and Python code. gitagent extracts the \u003cstrong\u003eidentity layer\u003c/strong\u003e — prompts, rules, roles, tool schemas — into a portable, versionable format.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat ports cleanly:\u003c/strong\u003e system prompts, persona definitions, hard constraints, tool schemas, role/SOD policies, model preferences.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat stays in the framework:\u003c/strong\u003e runtime orchestration (state machines, graph wiring), live tool execution, memory I/O, iterative loops.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis pattern is demonstrated with \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/NVIDIA-AI-Blueprints/aiq\"\u003eNVIDIA's AIQ Deep Researcher\u003c/a\u003e — a 3-agent hierarchy (orchestrator → planner → researcher) that produces cited research reports. The gitagent version captures the agent's identity, rules, and SOD policy so you can:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFork for a new domain\u003c/strong\u003e — edit \u003ccode\u003eSOUL.md\u003c/code\u003e for legal/medical/finance research without touching Python\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eVersion prompts independently\u003c/strong\u003e — \u003ccode\u003egit diff\u003c/code\u003e when the orchestrator's style regresses\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eValidate SOD\u003c/strong\u003e — \u003ccode\u003eopengap validate --compliance\u003c/code\u003e ensures the orchestrator can't also be the researcher\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExport to other runtimes\u003c/strong\u003e — same identity on Claude Code, OpenAI, or as a raw system prompt\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"examples/nvidia-deep-researcher/\n├── agent.yaml                  # Manifest + SOD policy\n├── SOUL.md                     # Orchestrator identity (from orchestrator.j2)\n├── RULES.md                    # Citation rules, report constraints\n├── DUTIES.md                   # Role separation: orchestrator ↔ planner ↔ researcher\n├── agents/planner/             # Planner sub-agent (from planner.j2)\n├── agents/researcher/          # Researcher sub-agent (from researcher.j2)\n├── skills/{web,paper,knowledge}-search/\n├── tools/*.yaml                # MCP-compatible tool schemas\n└── config/                     # Model assignments per environment\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eexamples/nvidia-deep-researcher/\n├── agent.yaml                  # Manifest + SOD policy\n├── SOUL.md                     # Orchestrator identity (from orchestrator.j2)\n├── RULES.md                    # Citation rules, report constraints\n├── DUTIES.md                   # Role separation: orchestrator ↔ planner ↔ researcher\n├── agents/planner/             # Planner sub-agent (from planner.j2)\n├── agents/researcher/          # Researcher sub-agent (from researcher.j2)\n├── skills/{web,paper,knowledge}-search/\n├── tools/*.yaml                # MCP-compatible tool schemas\n└── config/                     # Model assignments per environment\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSee \u003ca example.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eQuick Start\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca   <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/hero.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/hero.png" alt="OpenGAP — GitAgentProtocol (Open GAP)" width="700" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">OpenGAP | your repository becomes your agent</h1><a id="user-content-opengap--your-repository-becomes-your-agent" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: OpenGAP | your repository becomes your agent" href="#opengap--your-repository-becomes-your-agent"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>opengap</code></strong> — the OpenGAP CLI, published as <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@open-gitagent/opengap" rel="nofollow"><code>@open-gitagent/opengap</code></a>. Previously published as <code>@open-gitagent/gapman</code> and originally <code>@open-gitagent/gitagent</code>; the <code>gitagent</code> command is still installed as an alias for backward compatibility.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/@open-gitagent/opengap" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/19a2eed4d32ef67d58f93b4533cba587b7696a152d872c28f9779bd21394c717/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f406f70656e2d6769746167656e742f6f70656e676170" alt="npm version" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/@open-gitagent/opengap" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://github.com/open-gitagent/gitagent/actions/workflows/ci.yml"><img src="https://github.com/open-gitagent/gitagent/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg" alt="CI" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fdf2982b9f5d7489dcf44570e714e3a15fce6253e0cc6b5aa61a075aac2ff71b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4c6963656e73652d4d49542d79656c6c6f772e737667" alt="License: MIT" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-MIT-yellow.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://github.com/open-gitagent/gitagent/blob/main/spec/SPECIFICATION.md"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/84eb3c4cc1627b83d146643d9e30d94b541436f07c64378ac39c66c208d4ae8b/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f737065632d76302e312e302d626c7565" alt="Spec: v0.1.0" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/spec-v0.1.0-blue" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://nodejs.org" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a10dccd4c7701a4b9cc611567d49569029c5d8a338b11fe73b660061a7785324/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f6e6f64652d25334525334431382d627269676874677265656e" alt="Node &gt;= 18" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/node-%3E%3D18-brightgreen" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">OpenGAP (the Git Agent Protocol) is a framework-agnostic, git-native standard for defining AI agents. Clone a repo, get an agent. <code>opengap</code> is its reference CLI.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Why</h2><a id="user-content-why" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why" href="#why"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Every AI framework has its own structure. There's no universal, portable way to define an agent that works across Claude Code, OpenAI, LangChain, CrewAI, and AutoGen. <strong>gitagent</strong> fixes that.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Git-native</strong> — Version control, branching, diffing, and collaboration built in</li>
<li><strong>Framework-agnostic</strong> — Export to any framework with adapters</li>
<li><strong>Compliance-ready</strong> — First-class support for FINRA, Federal Reserve, SEC, and segregation of duties</li>
<li><strong>Composable</strong> — Agents can extend, depend on, and delegate to other agents</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The Standard</h2><a id="user-content-the-standard" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The Standard" href="#the-standard"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Your repository becomes your agent. Drop these files into any git repo and it becomes a portable, framework-agnostic agent definition — everything else (CLI, adapters, patterns) builds on top of it.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="my-agent/
│
│   # ── Core Identity (required) ──────────────────────────
├── agent.yaml              # Manifest — name, version, model, skills, tools, compliance
├── SOUL.md                 # Identity, personality, communication style, values
│
│   # ── Behavior &amp; Rules ──────────────────────────────────
├── RULES.md                # Hard constraints, must-always/must-never, safety boundaries
├── DUTIES.md               # Segregation of duties policy and role boundaries
├── AGENTS.md               # Framework-agnostic fallback instructions
│
│   # ── Capabilities ──────────────────────────────────────
├── skills/                 # Reusable capability modules (SKILL.md + scripts)
│   └── code-review/
│       ├── SKILL.md
│       └── review.sh
├── tools/                  # MCP-compatible tool definitions (YAML schemas)
├── workflows/              # Multi-step procedures/playbooks
│
│   # ── Knowledge &amp; Memory ────────────────────────────────
├── knowledge/              # Reference documents the agent can consult
├── memory/                 # Persistent cross-session memory
│   └── runtime/            # Live agent state (dailylog.md, context.md)
│
│   # ── Lifecycle &amp; Ops ───────────────────────────────────
├── hooks/                  # Lifecycle event handlers (bootstrap.md, teardown.md)
├── config/                 # Environment-specific overrides
├── compliance/             # Regulatory compliance artifacts
│
│   # ── Composition ───────────────────────────────────────
├── agents/                 # Sub-agent definitions (recursive structure)
│   └── fact-checker/
│       ├── agent.yaml
│       ├── SOUL.md
│       └── DUTIES.md       # This agent's role, permissions, boundaries
├── examples/               # Calibration interactions (few-shot)
│
│   # ── Runtime ───────────────────────────────────────────
└── .gitagent/              # Runtime state (gitignored)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>my-agent/
│

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Only two files are required: <strong><code>agent.yaml</code></strong> (the manifest) and <strong><code>SOUL.md</code></strong> (the identity). Everything else is optional — add what you need, ignore the rest.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Patterns</h2><a id="user-content-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Patterns" href="#patterns"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are the architectural patterns that emerge when you define agents as git-native file systems.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Human-in-the-Loop for RL Agents</h3><a id="user-content-human-in-the-loop-for-rl-agents" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Human-in-the-Loop for RL Agents" href="#human-in-the-loop-for-rl-agents"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When an agent learns a new skill or writes to memory, it opens a branch + PR for human review before merging.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/human-in-the-loop.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/human-in-the-loop.png" alt="Human-in-the-Loop" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segregation of Duties (SOD)</h3><a id="user-content-segregation-of-duties-sod" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Segregation of Duties (SOD)" href="#segregation-of-duties-sod"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">No single agent should control a critical process end-to-end. Define roles (<code>maker</code>, <code>checker</code>, <code>executor</code>, <code>auditor</code>), a conflict matrix (which roles can't be the same agent), and handoff workflows — all in <code>agent.yaml</code> + <code>DUTIES.md</code>. The validator catches violations before deployment.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="compliance:
  segregation_of_duties:
    roles:
      - id: maker
        description: Creates proposals
        permissions: [create, submit]
      - id: checker
        description: Reviews and approves
        permissions: [review, approve, reject]
    conflicts:
      - [maker, checker]         # maker cannot approve own work
    assignments:
      loan-originator: [maker]
      credit-reviewer: [checker]
    handoffs:
      - action: credit_decision
        required_roles: [maker, checker]
        approval_required: true
    enforcement: strict"><pre><span class="pl-ent">compliance</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">segregation_of_duties</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">roles</span>:
      - <span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">maker</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">Creates proposals</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">permissions</span>: <span class="pl-s">[create, submit]</span>
      - <span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">checker</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">Reviews and approves</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">permissions</span>: <span class="pl-s">[review, approve, reject]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">conflicts</span>:
      - <span class="pl-s">[maker, checker]         </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> maker cannot approve own work</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">assignments</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">loan-originator</span>: <span class="pl-s">[maker]</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">credit-reviewer</span>: <span class="pl-s">[checker]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">handoffs</span>:
      - <span class="pl-ent">action</span>: <span class="pl-s">credit_decision</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">required_roles</span>: <span class="pl-s">[maker, checker]</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">approval_required</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">enforcement</span>: <span class="pl-s">strict</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Live Agent Memory</h3><a id="user-content-live-agent-memory" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Live Agent Memory" href="#live-agent-memory"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>memory/</code> folder holds a <code>runtime/</code> subfolder where agents write live knowledge — <code>dailylog.md</code>, <code>key-decisions.md</code>, and <code>context.md</code> — persisting state across sessions.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/live-agent-memory.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/live-agent-memory.png" alt="Live Agent Memory" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Versioning</h3><a id="user-content-agent-versioning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Versioning" href="#agent-versioning"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Every change to your agent is a git commit. Roll back broken prompts, revert bad skills, and explore past versions — full undo history for your agent.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/agent-versioning.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/agent-versioning.png" alt="Agent Versioning" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Shared Context &amp; Skills via Monorepo</h3><a id="user-content-shared-context--skills-via-monorepo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Shared Context &amp; Skills via Monorepo" href="#shared-context--skills-via-monorepo"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Root-level <code>context.md</code>, <code>skills/</code>, <code>tools/</code> are automatically shared across every agent in the monorepo. No duplication, one source of truth.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/shared-context.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/shared-context.png" alt="Shared Context" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Branch-based Deployment</h3><a id="user-content-branch-based-deployment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Branch-based Deployment" href="#branch-based-deployment"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Use git branches (<code>dev</code> → <code>staging</code> → <code>main</code>) to promote agent changes through environments, just like shipping software.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/branch-deployment.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/branch-deployment.png" alt="Branch-based Deployment" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Knowledge Tree</h3><a id="user-content-knowledge-tree" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Knowledge Tree" href="#knowledge-tree"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>knowledge/</code> folder stores entity relationships as a hierarchical tree with embeddings, letting agents reason over structured data at runtime.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/knowledge-tree.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/knowledge-tree.png" alt="Knowledge Tree" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Forking &amp; Remixing</h3><a id="user-content-agent-forking--remixing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Forking &amp; Remixing" href="#agent-forking--remixing"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Fork any public agent repo, customize its <code>SOUL.md</code>, add your own skills, and PR improvements back upstream — open-source collaboration for AI agents.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/agent-forking.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/agent-forking.png" alt="Agent Forking &amp; Remixing" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CI/CD for Agents</h3><a id="user-content-cicd-for-agents" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CI/CD for Agents" href="#cicd-for-agents"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Run <code>opengap validate</code> on every push via GitHub Actions. Test agent behavior in CI, block bad merges, and auto-deploy — treat agent quality like code quality.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/ci-cd-agents.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/ci-cd-agents.png" alt="CI/CD for Agents" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Diff &amp; Audit Trail</h3><a id="user-content-agent-diff--audit-trail" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Diff &amp; Audit Trail" href="#agent-diff--audit-trail"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>git diff</code> shows exactly what changed between agent versions. <code>git blame</code> traces every line to who wrote it and when — full traceability out of the box.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/agent-diff-audit.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/agent-diff-audit.png" alt="Agent Diff &amp; Audit Trail" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tagged Releases</h3><a id="user-content-tagged-releases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tagged Releases" href="#tagged-releases"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tag stable agent versions like <code>v1.1.0</code>. Pin production to a tag, canary new versions on staging, and roll back instantly if something breaks.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/tagged-releases.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/tagged-releases.png" alt="Tagged Releases" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Secret Management via .gitignore</h3><a id="user-content-secret-management-via-gitignore" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Secret Management via .gitignore" href="#secret-management-via-gitignore"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Agent tools that need API keys read from a local <code>.env</code> file — kept out of version control via <code>.gitignore</code>. Agent config is shareable, secrets stay local.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/secret-management.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/secret-management.png" alt="Secret Management" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Lifecycle with Hooks</h3><a id="user-content-agent-lifecycle-with-hooks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Lifecycle with Hooks" href="#agent-lifecycle-with-hooks"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Define <code>bootstrap.md</code> and <code>teardown.md</code> in the <code>hooks/</code> folder to control what an agent does on startup and before it stops.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/patterns/agent-automation-hooks.png"><img src="/open-gitagent/opengap/raw/main/patterns/agent-automation-hooks.png" alt="Agent Lifecycle Hooks" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SkillsFlow</h3><a id="user-content-skillsflow" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SkillsFlow" href="#skillsflow"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Deterministic, multi-step workflows defined in <code>workflows/</code> as YAML. Chain <code>skill:</code>, <code>agent:</code>, and <code>tool:</code> steps with <code>depends_on</code> ordering, <code>${{ }}</code> template data flow, and per-step <code>prompt:</code> overrides. Every run follows the same path — no LLM discretion on execution order.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="name: code-review-flow
description: Full code review pipeline
triggers:
  - pull_request

steps:
  lint:
    skill: static-analysis
    inputs:
      path: ${{ trigger.changed_files }}

  review:
    agent: code-reviewer
    depends_on: [lint]
    prompt: |
      Focus on security and performance.
      Flag any use of eval() or raw SQL.
    inputs:
      findings: ${{ steps.lint.outputs.issues }}

  test:
    tool: bash
    depends_on: [lint]
    inputs:
      command: &quot;npm test -- --coverage&quot;

  report:
    skill: review-summary
    depends_on: [review, test]
    conditions:
      - ${{ steps.review.outputs.severity != 'none' }}
    inputs:
      review: ${{ steps.review.outputs.comments }}
      coverage: ${{ steps.test.outputs.report }}

error_handling:
  on_failure: notify
  channel: &quot;#eng-reviews&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">code-review-flow</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">Full code review pipeline</span>
<span class="pl-ent">triggers</span>:
  - <span class="pl-s">pull_request</span>

<span class="pl-ent">steps</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">lint</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">skill</span>: <span class="pl-s">static-analysis</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">inputs</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">${{ trigger.changed_files }}</span>

  <span class="pl-ent">review</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">agent</span>: <span class="pl-s">code-reviewer</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">depends_on</span>: <span class="pl-s">[lint]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">prompt</span>: <span class="pl-s">|</span>
<span class="pl-s">      Focus on security and performance.</span>
<span class="pl-s">      Flag any use of eval() or raw SQL.</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>    <span class="pl-ent">inputs</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">findings</span>: <span class="pl-s">${{ steps.lint.outputs.issues }}</span>

  <span class="pl-ent">test</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">tool</span>: <span class="pl-s">bash</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">depends_on</span>: <span class="pl-s">[lint]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">inputs</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">command</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>npm test -- --coverage<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-ent">report</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">skill</span>: <span class="pl-s">review-summary</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">depends_on</span>: <span class="pl-s">[review, test]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">conditions</span>:
      - <span class="pl-s">${{ steps.review.outputs.severity != 'none' }}</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">inputs</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">review</span>: <span class="pl-s">${{ steps.review.outputs.comments }}</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">coverage</span>: <span class="pl-s">${{ steps.test.outputs.report }}</span>

<span class="pl-ent">error_handling</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">on_failure</span>: <span class="pl-s">notify</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">channel</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>#eng-reviews<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Porting Framework Agents to GitAgent</h3><a id="user-content-porting-framework-agents-to-gitagent" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Porting Framework Agents to GitAgent" href="#porting-framework-agents-to-gitagent"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Agents built in frameworks like NVIDIA AIQ, LangGraph, or CrewAI have their identity split across config files, Jinja2 templates, and Python code. gitagent extracts the <strong>identity layer</strong> — prompts, rules, roles, tool schemas — into a portable, versionable format.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>What ports cleanly:</strong> system prompts, persona definitions, hard constraints, tool schemas, role/SOD policies, model preferences.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>What stays in the framework:</strong> runtime orchestration (state machines, graph wiring), live tool execution, memory I/O, iterative loops.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">This pattern is demonstrated with <a href="https://github.com/NVIDIA-AI-Blueprints/aiq">NVIDIA's AIQ Deep Researcher</a> — a 3-agent hierarchy (orchestrator → planner → researcher) that produces cited research reports. The gitagent version captures the agent's identity, rules, and SOD policy so you can:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Fork for a new domain</strong> — edit <code>SOUL.md</code> for legal/medical/finance research without touching Python</li>
<li><strong>Version prompts independently</strong> — <code>git diff</code> when the orchestrator's style regresses</li>
<li><strong>Validate SOD</strong> — <code>opengap validate --compliance</code> ensures the orchestrator can't also be the researcher</li>
<li><strong>Export to other runtimes</strong> — same identity on Claude Code, OpenAI, or as a raw system prompt</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="examples/nvidia-deep-researcher/
├── agent.yaml                  # Manifest + SOD policy
├── SOUL.md                     # Orchestrator identity (from orchestrator.j2)
├── RULES.md                    # Citation rules, report constraints
├── DUTIES.md                   # Role separation: orchestrator ↔ planner ↔ researcher
├── agents/planner/             # Planner sub-agent (from planner.j2)
├── agents/researcher/          # Researcher sub-agent (from researcher.j2)
├── skills/{web,paper,knowledge}-search/
├── tools/*.yaml                # MCP-compatible tool schemas
└── config/                     # Model assignments per environment"><pre class="notranslate"><code>examples/nvidia-deep-researcher/
├── agent.yaml                  # Manifest + SOD policy
├── SOUL.md                     # Orchestrator identity (from orchestrator.j2)
├── RULES.md                    # Citation rules, report constraints
├── DUTIES.md                   # Role separation: orchestrator ↔ planner ↔ researcher
├── agents/planner/             # Planner sub-agent (from planner.j2)
├── agents/researcher/          # Researcher sub-agent (from researcher.j2)
├── skills/{web,paper,knowledge}-search/
├── tools/*.yaml                # MCP-compatible tool schemas
└── config/                     # Model assignments per environment
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">See <a href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/examples/nvidia-deep-researcher"><code>examples/nvidia-deep-researcher/</code></a> for the full working example.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Install
npm i -g @open-gitagent/opengap

# Create a new agent
opengap init --template standard

# Validate
opengap validate

# View agent info
opengap info

# Export to system prompt
opengap export --format system-prompt"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Install</span>
npm i -g @open-gitagent/opengap

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Create a new agent</span>
opengap init --template standard

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Validate</span>
opengap validate

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> View agent info</span>
opengap info

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Export to system prompt</span>
opengap <span class="pl-k">export</span> --format system-prompt</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><code>gitagent</code> is installed as an alias — all <code>opengap &lt;cmd&gt;</code> calls work as <code>gitagent &lt;cmd&gt;</code> too.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">agent.yaml</h2><a id="user-content-agentyaml" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: agent.yaml" href="#agentyaml"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The only file with a strict schema. Minimal example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="spec_version: &quot;0.1.0&quot;
name: my-agent
version: 0.1.0
description: A helpful assistant agent"><pre><span class="pl-ent">spec_version</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0.1.0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">my-agent</span>
<span class="pl-ent">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">0.1.0</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">A helpful assistant agent</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Full example with compliance:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="spec_version: &quot;0.1.0&quot;
name: compliance-analyst
version: 1.0.0
description: Financial compliance analysis agent
model:
  preferred: claude-opus-4-6
compliance:
  risk_tier: high
  frameworks: [finra, federal_reserve, sec]
  supervision:
    human_in_the_loop: always
    kill_switch: true
  recordkeeping:
    audit_logging: true
    retention_period: 7y
    immutable: true
  model_risk:
    validation_cadence: quarterly
    ongoing_monitoring: true
  segregation_of_duties:
    roles:
      - id: analyst
        permissions: [create, submit]
      - id: reviewer
        permissions: [review, approve, reject]
    conflicts:
      - [analyst, reviewer]
    assignments:
      compliance-analyst: [analyst]
      fact-checker: [reviewer]
    enforcement: strict"><pre><span class="pl-ent">spec_version</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0.1.0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">compliance-analyst</span>
<span class="pl-ent">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">1.0.0</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">Financial compliance analysis agent</span>
<span class="pl-ent">model</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">preferred</span>: <span class="pl-s">claude-opus-4-6</span>
<span class="pl-ent">compliance</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">risk_tier</span>: <span class="pl-s">high</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">frameworks</span>: <span class="pl-s">[finra, federal_reserve, sec]</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">supervision</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">human_in_the_loop</span>: <span class="pl-s">always</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">kill_switch</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">recordkeeping</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">audit_logging</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">retention_period</span>: <span class="pl-c1">7y</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">immutable</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">model_risk</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">validation_cadence</span>: <span class="pl-s">quarterly</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">ongoing_monitoring</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">segregation_of_duties</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">roles</span>:
      - <span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">analyst</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">permissions</span>: <span class="pl-s">[create, submit]</span>
      - <span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">reviewer</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">permissions</span>: <span class="pl-s">[review, approve, reject]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">conflicts</span>:
      - <span class="pl-s">[analyst, reviewer]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">assignments</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">compliance-analyst</span>: <span class="pl-s">[analyst]</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">fact-checker</span>: <span class="pl-s">[reviewer]</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">enforcement</span>: <span class="pl-s">strict</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CLI Commands</h2><a id="user-content-cli-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CLI Commands" href="#cli-commands"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Both <code>opengap</code> and <code>gitagent</code> refer to the same binary — use whichever you prefer.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Command</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap init [--template]</code></td>
<td>Scaffold new agent (<code>minimal</code>, <code>standard</code>, <code>full</code>, <code>llm-wiki</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap validate [--compliance]</code></td>
<td>Validate against spec and regulatory requirements</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap info</code></td>
<td>Display agent summary</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap export --format &lt;fmt&gt;</code></td>
<td>Export to other formats (see adapters below)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap import --from &lt;fmt&gt; &lt;path&gt;</code></td>
<td>Import (<code>claude</code>, <code>cursor</code>, <code>crewai</code>, <code>opencode</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap run &lt;source&gt; --adapter &lt;a&gt;</code></td>
<td>Run an agent from a git repo or local directory</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap install</code></td>
<td>Resolve and install git-based dependencies</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap audit</code></td>
<td>Generate compliance audit report</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap skills &lt;cmd&gt;</code></td>
<td>Manage skills (<code>search</code>, <code>install</code>, <code>list</code>, <code>info</code>)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>opengap lyzr &lt;cmd&gt;</code></td>
<td>Manage Lyzr agents (<code>create</code>, <code>update</code>, <code>info</code>, <code>run</code>)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compliance</h2><a id="user-content-compliance" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compliance" href="#compliance"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">gitagent has first-class support for financial regulatory compliance:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">FINRA</h3><a id="user-content-finra" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: FINRA" href="#finra"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Rule 3110</strong> — Supervision: human-in-the-loop, escalation triggers, kill switch</li>
<li><strong>Rule 4511</strong> — Recordkeeping: immutable audit logs, retention periods, SEC 17a-4 compliance</li>
<li><strong>Rule 2210</strong> — Communications: fair/balanced enforcement, no misleading statements</li>
<li><strong>Reg Notice 24-09</strong> — Existing rules apply to GenAI/LLMs</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Federal Reserve</h3><a id="user-content-federal-reserve" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Federal Reserve" href="#federal-reserve"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>SR 11-7</strong> — Model Risk Management: validation cadence, ongoing monitoring, outcomes analysis</li>
<li><strong>SR 23-4</strong> — Third-Party Risk: vendor due diligence, SOC reports, subcontractor assessment</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SEC / CFPB</h3><a id="user-content-sec--cfpb" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: SEC / CFPB" href="#sec--cfpb"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Reg S-P</strong> — Customer privacy, PII handling</li>
<li><strong>CFPB Circular 2022-03</strong> — Explainable adverse action, Less Discriminatory Alternative search</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segregation of Duties</h3><a id="user-content-segregation-of-duties" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Segregation of Duties" href="#segregation-of-duties"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Roles &amp; Permissions</strong> — Define maker, checker, executor, auditor roles with controlled permissions</li>
<li><strong>Conflict Matrix</strong> — Declare which role pairs cannot be held by the same agent</li>
<li><strong>Handoff Workflows</strong> — Require multi-agent participation for critical actions (credit decisions, regulatory filings)</li>
<li><strong>Isolation</strong> — Full state and credential segregation between roles</li>
<li><strong>DUTIES.md</strong> — Root-level policy + per-agent role declarations</li>
<li><strong>Enforcement</strong> — Strict (blocks deployment) or advisory (warnings only)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Inspired by <a href="https://www.trysalient.com/" rel="nofollow">Salient AI</a>'s purpose-built agent architecture and the <a href="https://air-governance-framework.finos.org/mitigations/mi-22_multi-agent-isolation-and-segmentation.html" rel="nofollow">FINOS AI Governance Framework</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Run <code>opengap audit</code> for a full compliance checklist against your agent configuration.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adapters</h2><a id="user-content-adapters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adapters" href="#adapters"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Adapters are used by both <code>export</code> and <code>run</code>. Available adapters:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Export to system prompt
opengap export --format system-prompt

# Run an agent directly
opengap run ./my-agent --adapter lyzr

# Run an agent definition against a separate target workspace
opengap run --dir ./agents/reviewer --workspace ~/code/my-app --adapter claude -p &quot;Review this repository&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Export to system prompt</span>
opengap <span class="pl-k">export</span> --format system-prompt

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run an agent directly</span>
opengap run ./my-agent --adapter lyzr

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run an agent definition against a separate target workspace</span>
opengap run --dir ./agents/reviewer --workspace <span class="pl-k">~</span>/code/my-app --adapter claude -p <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Review this repository<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inheritance &amp; Composition</h2><a id="user-content-inheritance--composition" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inheritance &amp; Composition" href="#inheritance--composition"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Extend a parent agent
extends: https://github.com/org/base-agent.git

# Compose with dependencies
dependencies:
  - name: fact-checker
    source: https://github.com/org/fact-checker.git
    version: ^1.0.0
    mount: agents/fact-checker"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Extend a parent agent</span>
<span class="pl-ent">extends</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://github.com/org/base-agent.git</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Compose with dependencies</span>
<span class="pl-ent">dependencies</span>:
  - <span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">fact-checker</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">source</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://github.com/org/fact-checker.git</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">version</span>: <span class="pl-s">^1.0.0</span>
    <span class="pl-ent">mount</span>: <span class="pl-s">agents/fact-checker</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Examples</h2><a id="user-content-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Examples" href="#examples"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See the <code>examples/</code> directory:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>examples/minimal/</code></strong> — 2-file hello world (agent.yaml + SOUL.md)</li>
<li><strong><code>examples/standard/</code></strong> — Code review agent with skills, tools, and rules</li>
<li><strong><code>examples/full/</code></strong> — Production compliance agent with all directories, hooks, workflows, sub-agents, SOD with DUTIES.md, and regulatory artifacts</li>
<li><strong><code>examples/gitagent-helper/</code></strong> — Helper agent that assists with creating gitagent definitions</li>
<li><strong><code>examples/lyzr-agent/</code></strong> — Example Lyzr Studio integration</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Specification</h2><a id="user-content-specification" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Specification" href="#specification"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Full specification at <a href="/open-gitagent/opengap/blob/main/spec/SPECIFICATION.md"><code>spec/SPECIFICATION.md</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">JSON Schemas for validation at <code>spec/schemas/</code>.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Built with gitagent?</h2><a id="user-content-built-with-gitagent" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Built with gitagent?" href="#built-with-gitagent"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you've built an agent using gitagent, we'd love to hear about it! <a href="https://github.com/open-gitagent/gitagent/discussions">Open a discussion</a> or add a <code>gitagent</code> topic to your repo.</p>
